<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjažólyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>вес</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ves</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжеловесный.html>тяжелове́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjaželovésnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тяжелове́снее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тяжелове́сней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heavy, weighty</li>
<li>massive, cumbersome</li>
<li>graceless, unsubtle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">technical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heavyweight
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжеловесный.html>тяжелове́сный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tjaželovésnyj</b> pójezd</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>heavyweight</b> train</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тяжелый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлый</a> (389)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęželъ</i>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжкий.html>тя́жкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjážkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see there for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjažólyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)тяжеле́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелеть.html>тяжеле́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелейший.html>тяжеле́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heavy</li>
<li>difficult, hard</li>
<li>laborious</li>
<li>serious</li>
<li>severe, grave</li>
<li>grievous, oppressive, painful, sad</li></ol>

<p><b>тя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жё<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лый</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жесть</a> (2490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжкий.html>тя́жкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjážkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жесть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjážestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жести</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жести</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тяжесть.html>тя́жестей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>heaviness</li>
<li>weight</li>
<li>load</li>
<li>burden</li>
<li>gravity</li>
<li>seriousness</li>
<li>painfulness</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжкий.html>тя́жкий</a> (4225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">тѧжькъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tęžĭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęžьkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>hard, grave</li>
<li>terrible, painful</li></ol>

***тянуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a> (1323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tęgnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потянуть.html>потяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to pull, to draw, to haul, to drag</li>
<li>to lay (a cable)</li>
<li>to draw (a wire)</li>
<li>to drawl, to drag out <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">speak slowly</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to drag out, to delay, to protract, to procrastinate</li>
<li>to make someone go, to force to go</li>
<li>to weigh</li>
<li>to draw up</li>
<li>to squeeze, to extort</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be drawn to, to long for, to miss
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1986</b>,  Сергей Донатович Довлатов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sergei_Dovlatov" class="extiw" title="w:Sergei Dovlatov">Sergei Donatovich Dovlatov</a>),  “Куртка Фернана Леже  | Fernand Léger's Jacket | ”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:чемодан.html>Чемода́н</a></cite>  | <cite>The Suitcase</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сознательный.html>созна́тельную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:инстинктивный.html>инстинкти́вно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ущербный.html>уще́рбным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́дям</a> - <a href = vnd.unilang:бедняк.html>бедняка́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:хулиган.html>хулига́нам</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:начинающий.html>начина́ющим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́там</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsju soznátelʹnuju žiznʹ menjá instinktívno <b>tjanúlo</b> k uščérbnym ljúdjam - bednjakám, xuligánam, načinájuščim poétam.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">My whole conscious life I have instinctively been <b>drawn</b> to damaged people: paupers, hooligans, beginning poets.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>

<p><b>тя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3c.
<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ниях</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:веять.html>ве́ять</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>стано́вится</a> непереходным. <a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> малоупотребительная <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> деепричастия <i>тяня́</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-тя-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тяну́ться</a> (1791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потянуться.html>потяну́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:протянуться.html>протяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stretch</li>
<li>to stretch out, to stretch oneself</li>
<li>to stretch, to extend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:километр.html>киломе́тров</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тя́нется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тайга.html>тайга́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po tu stóronu na sótni kilométrov <b>tjánetsja</b> tajgá</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">on that side for hundreds of kilometres stretches the taiga</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drag on; to crawl, to hang heavy</li>
<li>to last out, to hold out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тя́нутся</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapásy ješčó <b>tjánutsja</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">supplies are still holding out</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to reach (for), to reach out (for); to strive (after)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуться.html>тяну́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ве</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tjanútʹsja</b> k sláve</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strive after fame</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drift</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>тя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. ***тятя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тятя.html>тя́тя</a> (23770)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tetę</i>, cf. <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:тата.html>та́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">táto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тятя.html>тя́тя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tjátja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тятя.html>тя́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тятя.html>тя́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тятя.html>тя́тей</a></b>)

Зализняка).

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*u</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_3">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">u</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>at, by, near
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окна́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>u</b> okná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the window</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>оте́ц</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сын.html>сы́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Otéc <b>u</b> sýna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The father is at his son’s (house).</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in the possession of <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">used to express "to have"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>каранда́ш</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>U</b> vas jestʹ karandáš?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Do you have a pencil?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>карандаша́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>U</b> menjá net karandašá.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don’t have a pencil.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:убавивший.html>уба́вивший</a></b>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ба́вить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-bávitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убегавший.html>убега́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubegávšij</span>)

***убегать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убегать.html>убега́ть</a> (4642)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убегать.html>убега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run away, to make off, to flee</li>
<li>to escape</li>
<li>to boil over (of liquid)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:убегать.html>убега́ет</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">molokó <b>ubegájet</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the milk is boiling over</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:гать.html>га́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.    <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>Образова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> 1-го <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднённый.html>затруднено́</a>.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:убеждать.html>убежда́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:убедить.html>убеди́ть</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> реципиент (<a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. п.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/25/NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-3.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:обстоятельство.html>обстоя́тельство</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> + предл. п.).

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убедиться.html>убеди́ться</a> (1889)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убедить.html>убеди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ubedítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убедиться.html>убеди́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubedítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убеждаться.html>убежда́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be convinced, to receive evidence</li>
<li>to make sure, to make certain</li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4b.    <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>Образова́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> 1-го <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:затруднённый.html>затруднено́</a>.  <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:убеждаться.html>убежда́ться</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-убед-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***убежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́ть</a> (2863)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">у-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убегать.html>убега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run away, to make off, to flee</li>
<li>to escape</li>
<li>to boil over (of liquid)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">molokó <b>ubežálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the milk has boiled over</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жа́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>беж<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>да́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ние</a> (4290)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubeždénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убеждение.html>убежде́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>belief, conviction</li>
<li>persuasion <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the act of persuading</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежденность.html>убеждённость</a> (15331)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убедить.html>убеждённый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ubeždjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жище</a> (5975)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежать.html>убежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ubežátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to flee</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ище</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-išče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жище</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ubéžišče</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жища</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жища</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:убежище.html>убе́жищ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>asylum, refuge, sanctuary (a state of safety, protection or shelter)</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>бе́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>жи<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ще</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 4a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>у-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-беж-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стойбище.html>-ищ</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
